Passive Noble Mind
Master Level 6
Description Enhances Empress's Blessing effects.
Level 1 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 1
6 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 6
Passive Noble Mind
Master Level 6
Description Enhances Empress's Blessing effects.
Level 1 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 1
2 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 2
3 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 3
4 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 4
5 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 5
6 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 6


Active Hero's Echo
Master Level 1
Description [Master Level: 1]
Increases the Attack Power and Magic ATT of all nearby players.
Cooldown: 300 sec
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Attack Power and Magic ATT: + 4%, Duration: 40 min


Active Elemental Slash
Master Level 1
Description Attack enemies in front of you with pure, primal energy.
Level 1 MP Cost: 0, Damage: 130%, Number of Attacks: 1, Max Enemies Hit: 3


Active Imperial Recall
Master Level 1
Description Return to the Empress using Shinsoo's power.
Level 1 MP Cost: 100, return to Ereve immediately.
Cooldown: 600 sec.


Passive Elemental Harmony
Master Level 1
Description Use the harmony of nature to build affinity for an element of your choosing.
Level 1 Strength increases 1 for every 2 levels the character gains


Passive Elemental Expert
Master Level 1
Description Become an expert of the elements to increase Attack Power and Magic ATT.
Level 1 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +10%


Passive Elemental Shift
Master Level 1
Description Jump in any direction except down by pressing a direction key and jump in midair.
Level 1 MP Cost: 4, jumps further in the appropriate direction
Show/hide all levels
Passive Cygnus Blessing (Warrior)
Master Level 10
Description Blessings from an awakened Empress Cygnus protect you from harm.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 5 times, once for each unique Cygnus Knights job character you have on this world.
Level 1 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +7, Abnormal Status Resistance: +1, All Elemental Resistance: +1%
10 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +25, Abnormal Status Resistance: +15, All Elemental Resistance: +15%

The Basics of a Dawn Warrior

Show/hide all levels
Active Rising Sun
Master Level 10
Description Allows you to use Solar skills by putting the power of sunlight in the sword.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 10 required to learn Equinox Cycle.
Rising Sun/Falling Moon Character Stance Lock: Right-click
Level 1 Final Damage: +5%, Attack Speed: +1
Cannot be used at the same time as Falling Moon.
10 Final Damage: +10%, Attack Speed: +1
Cannot be used at the same time as Falling Moon.

Show/hide all levels
Active Falling Moon
Master Level 10
Description Allows you to use Luna skills by receiving the power of the moonlight in the sword. Does not apply to summoning skills, 5th Job Common Skills, or certain other skills. SP is not required for this skill, and it follows the skill level of Rising Sun.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 10 required to learn Equinox Cycle.
Level 1 Critical Rate: +1%
Number of Attacks for Skills: x2, Final Damage is decreased to 51%
Number of attacks cannot exceed 15.
Cannot be used at the same time as Rising Sun.
10 Critical Rate: +10%
Number of Attacks for Skills: x2, Final Damage is decreased to 55%
Number of attacks cannot exceed 15.
Cannot be used at the same time as Rising Sun.

Level 20 required to learn Celestial Vision.

Active Soul Element
Master Level 10
Description Summons a light element to gain its power. Chance to obtain cosmic orb when the Solar/Luna skill opposite to the previous skill that hit the target also lands a hit. Temporarily increases Attack Power when cosmic orb is created.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 10 required to learn Soul Blessing.
Level 1 When the Solar/Luna skill opposite to the previous skill that hit the target also lands a hit, 32% chance to create 1 cosmic orb that lasts 30 sec
Max Cosmic Orb Stacks: 2, duration of all cosmic orbs reset upon creation
When cosmic orb is created, Attack Power increases by 11 for 30 sec
[Passive Effect: Ignore Enemy Defense: 1%]
10 When the Solar/Luna skill opposite to the previous skill that hit the target also lands a hit, 50% chance to create 1 cosmic orb that lasts 30 sec
Max Cosmic Orb Stacks: 2, duration of all cosmic orbs reset upon creation
When cosmic orb is created, Attack Power increases by 20 for 30 sec
[Passive Effect: Ignore Enemy Defense: 10%]
Active Soul Element
Master Level 10
Description Summons a light element to gain its power. Chance to obtain cosmic orb when the Solar/Luna skill opposite to the previous skill that hit the target also lands a hit. Temporarily increases Attack Power when cosmic orb is created.

Active Soul Leap
Master Level 1
Description Leap once more while already in the air. Press the up key at the same to move upward.
SP is not required for this skill, and it can be used upon job advancing to Dawn Warrior.
Level 1 MP Cost: 5. Allows you to jump a greater distance.

Description Enhance your swordsmanship with celestial energy.

Active Cosmic Matter
Master Level 20
Description [Cosmic]
Launches a condensed dark matter in front. If the dark matter attacks all attackable targets or reaches max range, it explodes to deal damage to nearby enemies. Consumes all cosmic orbs upon use, and deals more powerful damage based on the number of cosmic orbs consumed.
Required Skill: Soul Element Lv. 10
Level 1 MP Cost: 15, consumes all cosmic orbs and launches a dark matter.
Dark Matter - Max Enemies Pierced: 8, Damage: 122%, Number of Attacks: 2. Upon exploding, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 163%, Number of Attacks: 3
Dark Matter Damage per Cosmic Orb Consumed: +20% points
Cooldown: 15 sec
20 MP Cost: 25, consumes all cosmic orbs and launches a dark matter.
Dark Matter - Max Enemies Pierced: 8, Damage: 160%, Number of Attacks: 2. Upon exploding, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 220%, Number of Attacks: 3
Dark Matter Damage per Cosmic Orb Consumed: +20% points
Cooldown: 15 sec
Active Cosmic Matter
Master Level 20
Description [Cosmic]

Active Equinox Cycle
Master Level 10
Description Reconfigures the solar and lunar cycles to automatically change stances when using Solar/Luna skills. Additionally enhances the effect of Rising Sun and Falling Moon. Overwrites the effect of Rising Sun and Falling Moon.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Required Skill: Rising Sun/Falling Moon Lv. 10
Level 10 required to learn 3rd job skill Equinox Mastery and 4th job skill Equinox Slash.
Right-click to lock activation effect.
Level 1 MP Cost: 31, changes stance every time Solar/Luna skills are used
Rising Sun - Final Damage: +11%, Attack Speed: +1
Falling Moon - Critical Rate: +10%, Number of Attacks for Skills: x2, Final Damage is decreased to 56%
Number of attacks cannot exceed 15.
10 MP Cost: 35, changes stance every time Solar/Luna skills are used
Rising Sun - Final Damage: +15%, Attack Speed: +1
Falling Moon - Critical Rate: +15%, Number of Attacks for Skills: x2, Final Damage is decreased to 60%
Number of attacks cannot exceed 15.

Active Cosmic Shower
Master Level 20
Description [Cosmic]
Uses the dormant power in the orbs to create a meteor shower zone that continuously attacks the surroundings for a set time. Consumes all cosmic orbs upon use, and duration increases based on the number of cosmic orbs consumed. Cosmic Shower can be used without casting motion during Solar Slash, Luna Divide, and Styx Crossing. The duration of Cosmic Shower doesn't increase with the summons duration increase, and is unaffected by attack reflection. The attack count increase effect of Falling Moon doesn't apply.
Required Skill: Soul Element Lv. 10
Level 1 MP Cost: 35, consumes all cosmic orbs to create meteor shower zone
Meteor Shower Zone - Duration: 45 sec, Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 153%, Number of Attacks: 3
Meteor Shower Duration per Cosmic Orb Consumed: +3 sec
Damage Against Normal Enemies: +50%
Cooldown: 30 sec
20 MP Cost: 45, consumes all cosmic orbs to create meteor shower zone
Meteor Shower Zone - Duration: 45 sec, Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 210%, Number of Attacks: 3
Meteor Shower Duration per Cosmic Orb Consumed: +3 sec
Damage Against Normal Enemies: +50%
Cooldown: 30 sec

Active Cosmic Burst
Master Level 30
Description [Cosmic]
Releases cosmic orbs to attack. Consumes all cosmic orbs upon use, and decreases cooldown based on the number of cosmic orbs consumed. Cosmic Burst can be used without casting motion during Solar Slash, Luna Divide, and Styx Crossing. The released cosmic orbs target the boss with the highest HP first, and is unaffected by attack reflection. Cosmic Burst is not affected by effects which reset or reduce cooldown.
In Auto Mode, Cosmic Burst is used automatically when it's not on cooldown and cosmic orb is at max, upon landing Solar Slash, Luna Divide, or Styx Crossing.
Required Skill: Soul Element Lv. 10
Auto Mode On/Off: Right-click
Level 1 MP Cost: 35, releases cosmic orb by consuming all cosmic orbs
Each of the released cosmic orbs targets 1 enemy, Damage: 305%, Number of Attacks: 4
If a single enemy gets hit with several cosmic orbs, Final Damage is decreased by 30% starting with the second orb.
Cooldown per Cosmic Orb Consumed: -1 sec

[Passive Effect: Cosmic Shower Damage: +62% points]
Active Cosmic Burst
Master Level 30
Description [Cosmic]
Releases cosmic orbs to attack. Consumes all cosmic orbs upon use, and decreases cooldown based on the number of cosmic orbs consumed. Cosmic Burst can be used without casting motion during Solar Slash, Luna Divide, and Styx Crossing. The released cosmic orbs target the boss with the highest HP first, and is unaffected by attack reflection. Cosmic Burst is not affected by effects which reset or reduce cooldown.
In Auto Mode, Cosmic Burst is used automatically when it's not on cooldown and cosmic orb is at max, upon landing Solar Slash, Luna Divide, or Styx Crossing.
Required Skill: Soul Element Lv. 10
Auto Mode On/Off: Right-click
Level 1 MP Cost: 35, releases cosmic orb by consuming all cosmic orbs
Each of the released cosmic orbs targets 1 enemy, Damage: 305%, Number of Attacks: 4
If a single enemy gets hit with several cosmic orbs, Final Damage is decreased by 30% starting with the second orb.
Cooldown per Cosmic Orb Consumed: -1 sec

Active Blazing Assault
Level Requirement 160
Master Level 1
Description [Solar]
Moves while instantly cutting enemies with the sword enveloped in the sun's flame. Become temporarily invincible upon use. Shares cooldown with Luster Charge, and can be used by linking with Luster Charge once regardless of the stance within a set time after casting. If you linked from Luster Charge, you cannot link to Luster Charge. Stance does not change due to Equinox Cycle.
Required Skill: Rising Sun/Falling Moon Lv. 1
Level 1 MP Cost: 100, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 400%, Number of Attacks: 6
After casting, Invincibility Duration: 1.8 sec, can link with Luster Charge within 5 sec
Cooldown: 45 sec

Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF

Cooldown: 60 sec

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec

Active True Arachnid Reflection
Master Level 25
Description The collapsing space between the Mirror World and reality become linked with Will's Erda, causing the spider within the mirror to temporarily materialize in reality.
Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP
Spatial Collapse - Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 468%, Number of Attacks: 15, Once complete, summons True Arachnid Reflection.
True Arachnid Reflection - Duration: 50 sec, Goes into attack mode at set intervals. During attack mode, uses spider legs 10 times to deal 182% damage 8 times. If the spider legs attack one target 5 consecutive times, attack mode will end immediately. 3 sec cooldown after attack mode ends.
Cooldown: 250 sec

Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP
Spatial Collapse - Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 468%, Number of Attacks: 15, Once complete, summons True Arachnid Reflection.
True Arachnid Reflection - Duration: 50 sec, Goes into attack mode at set intervals. During attack mode, uses spider legs 10 times to deal 182% damage 8 times. If the spider legs attack one target 5 consecutive times, attack mode will end immediately. 3 sec cooldown after attack mode ends.
Cooldown: 250 sec

Active Solar Crest
Master Level 25
Description Mitra's power manifests the searing heat of the sun as a blazing inferno. The flame emblem is unaffected by attack reflection and disappears when you change maps.
Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP
Mitra's Fire: summons a Flame Emblem after dealing 780% damage up to 15 enemies 12 times.
Flame Emblem: deals 208% damage to up to 2 enemies 6 times every 2.1 sec for 51 sec. Deals 286% damage if striking a single enemy.
Cooldown: 250 sec
25 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP
Mitra's Fire: summons a Flame Emblem after dealing 1500% damage up to 15 enemies 12 times.
Flame Emblem: deals 400% damage to up to 2 enemies 6 times every 2.1 sec for 51 sec. Deals 550% damage if striking a single enemy.
Cooldown: 250 sec
30 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP
Mitra's Fire: summons a Flame Emblem after dealing 1650% damage up to 15 enemies 12 times.
Flame Emblem: deals 440% damage to up to 2 enemies 6 times every 2.1 sec for 51 sec. Deals 605% damage if striking a single enemy.
Cooldown: 250 sec

Active Phalanx Charge
Master Level 25
Description Summons brave Spearmen of the Cygnus Knights to charge enemies in a phalanx formation. The spearmen slow down upon touching an enemy. Press the skill key again to change their direction of movement. Unaffected by attack reflection and can be resisted by some monsters.
Level 1 MP Cost: 500, Damage: 468%, Number of Attacks: 41
Spearmen disappear when the number of attacks is reached, they move a certain distance, or after a certain duration. Activate the skill again to change their direction.
Cooldown: 30 sec
25 MP Cost: 500, Damage: 900%, Number of Attacks: 65
Spearmen disappear when the number of attacks is reached, they move a certain distance, or after a certain duration. Activate the skill again to change their direction.
Cooldown: 30 sec
30 MP Cost: 500, Damage: 990%, Number of Attacks: 70
Spearmen disappear when the number of attacks is reached, they move a certain distance, or after a certain duration. Activate the skill again to change their direction.
Cooldown: 30 sec

Class-Specific Skills

Active Rift of Damnation
Master Level 25
Description Creates a rift between the world of the living and the Underworld when used with Styx Crossing. You can use Styx Crossing with a regular attack while Rift of Damnation is active. Using Action Customization allows you to use Styx Crossing with a regular attack or Solar Slash/Luna Divide. Styx Crossing and the attack from the rift is unaffected by attack reflection.
Action Customization On/Off: Right-click
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, creates max cosmic orbs upon use, Styx Crossing can be used for 40 sec
Styx Crossing - Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 395%, Number of Attacks: 5, Number of Chase Cuts: 5. Additional Ignore Enemy Defense: +20%, creates max cosmic orbs, changes stance with Equinox Cycle
Attacking with Styx Crossing cuts space to leave a rift for 10 sec
Rift - Gradually grows when it's attacked by Styx Crossing and in the end, Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 541%, Number of Attacks: 6, Number of Explosions: 5
More than 2 rifts cannot be created at the same. Rift can be created again in 5 sec after exploding. Rift disappears and explodes immediately when duration ends but damage is decreased.
Cooldown: 180 sec
25 MP Cost: 1000, creates max cosmic orbs upon use, Styx Crossing can be used for 40 sec

Rift - Gradually grows when it's attacked by Styx Crossing and in the end, Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 1045%, Number of Attacks: 6, Number of Explosions: 5
More than 2 rifts cannot be created at the same. Rift can be created again in 5 sec after exploding. Rift disappears and explodes immediately when duration ends but damage is decreased.
Cooldown: 180 sec

Active Soul Eclipse
Master Level 25
Description Focus your wisdom and the strength of your soul to call forth a stunning eclipse. When the sun and the moon completely overlap, use the skill one more time to use Equinox Divide. Equinox Divide can be used while attacking with Solar Slash, Luna Divide, and Styx Crossing. The eclipse is unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, creates an eclipse, attacking up to15 enemies 7 time(s), dealing 468% damage 40 times consecutively. Invincible during casting.
Equinox Divide: The eclipse dissipates, triggering explosions 5 time(s) at a certain interval. Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 1300%, Number of Attacks: 15. Invincible while casting. If you use in the air, you can use it while using an attack skill in mid-air.
Cooldown: 180 sec.

Master Level 25
Description Unleash an explosive eruption of forged Spiritual Resin. Activates when your attack skill hits while in Falling Moon or Rising Sun stances. Cooldown is reduced when stance is changed with Equinox Cycle or Styx Crossing hits. Flare Slash is unaffected by attack reflection and cooldown reduction.

Active Astral Blitz
Master Level 30
Description A sword forged from your own soul cuts the formless space to reproduce the Big Bang.

Lv. 10: Ignore Defense +20%
Lv. 20: Boss Damage +20%
Lv. 30: Ignore Defense +30% and Boss Damage +30%
Level 1 MP Cost: 1200, invincible during casting
Chase Cut occurs 48 times which attack up to 15 enemies with 1085% damage 5 times
After that, triggers 24 Big Bang that attack up to 15 enemies for 1076% damage 7 times.
Increases final damage by 5% for 20 seconds when used
Cooldown: 360 sec
30 MP Cost: 1200, invincible during casting
Chase Cut occurs 48 times which attack up to 15 enemies with 2100% damage 5 times
After that, triggers 24 Big Bang that attack up to 15 enemies for 2062% damage 7 times.
Increases final damage by 10% for 20 seconds when used
Cooldown: 360 sec

Active Equinox Power
Master Level 30
Description Detonate the power that lies within the merged celestial body,
consecutively activating the sword energy of blinding sun rays and the cold moonlight.
Activates automatically if Equinox Power is not on cooldown when landing Solar Slash,
Luna Divide, or Styx Crossing.
Unaffected by attack reflection.

Cooldown: 20 sec

Active HEXA Cosmic Shower
Master Level 30
Description [Cosmic]
Use the dormant power in the orbs to create a meteor shower zone that continuously attacks the surroundings for a set time. Consume all cosmic orbs upon use, and duration increases based on the number of cosmic orbs consumed. Cosmic Shower can be used without casting motion during Solar Slash, Luna Divide, and Styx Crossing.
The duration of Cosmic Shower doesn't increase with the summons duration increase, and is unaffected by attack reflection.
The attack count increase effect of Falling Moon doesn't apply.
Required Skill: #Cosmic Shower Lv. 20
Level 1 MP Cost: 35, consume all cosmic orbs to create meteor shower zone
Meteor Shower Zone - Duration: 45 sec, Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 305%, Number of Attacks: 3
Meteor Shower Duration per Cosmic Orb Consumed: +3 sec
Damage Against Normal Enemies: +50%
Cooldown: 30 sec
30 MP Cost: 45, consume all cosmic orbs to create meteor shower zone
Meteor Shower Zone - Duration: 45 sec, Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 740%, Number of Attacks: 3
Meteor Shower Duration per Cosmic Orb Consumed: +3 sec
Damage Against Normal Enemies: +50%
Cooldown: 30 sec

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
